static MONKEY_FILE: &[u8; 69624] = include_bytes!("../../tset/monkey.meenle_noonle_mesh");

pub fn monkey() -> Mesh {
    // SAFETY: no
    let monkey_tris = unsafe { *((*MONKEY_FILE).as_ptr().cast::<[Tri; 967]>()) };
    Mesh::from(Vec::from(monkey_tris))
}

pub fn icosphere() -> Mesh {
    Mesh::from(Vec::from(ICOSPHERE_TRIS))
}
